Browse by Incipit

The following index gives access to all TML texts from their incipits. Note that longer treatises are split into parts, usually chapters, and incipits are given for all parts.

Expand a line to show the details and access the texts.

      Source: Adrien de la Fage, Essais de dipthérographie musicale (Paris: Legouix, 1864), 355–62.

  • [+] Viso igitur, quid sit discantus, quaedam precognitiones sunt videndae.

    • Anonymous – Discantus positio vulgaris (dispovu)

      Source: Hieronymus de Moravia, Tractatus de musica, ed. S. M. Cserba, Freiburger Studien zur Musikwissenschaft, vol. 2 (Regensburg: Pustet, 1935), 189–94.

  • [+] Viso igitur quid sit discantus, quedam precognitiones sunt vidende.

    • Anonymous – Discantus positio vulgaris (dispos)

    • Anonymous – Species plani cantus sunt terdecim (anospe)

    • Anonymous – [Ad organum faciendum] (adorfba)
